        <div data-pjax="true" data-test-selector="body-content" data-view-component="true" class="markdown-body tmp-my-3"><h2>What's changed</h2>
<ul>
<li>Added MCP elicitation support — MCP servers can now request structured input mid-task via an interactive dialog (form fields or browser URL)</li>
<li>Added new <code>Elicitation</code> and <code>ElicitationResult</code> hooks to intercept and override responses before they're sent back</li>
<li>Added <code>-n</code> / <code>--name &lt;name&gt;</code> CLI flag to set a display name for the session at startup</li>
<li>Added <code>worktree.sparsePaths</code> setting for <code>claude --worktree</code> in large monorepos to check out only the directories you need via git sparse-checkout</li>
<li>Added <code>PostCompact</code> hook that fires after compaction completes</li>
<li>Added <code>/effort</code> slash command to set model effort level</li>
<li>Added session quality survey — enterprise admins can configure the sample rate via the <code>feedbackSurveyRate</code> setting</li>
<li>Fixed deferred tools (loaded via <code>ToolSearch</code>) losing their input schemas after conversation compaction, causing array and number parameters to be rejected with type errors</li>
<li>Fixed slash commands showing "Unknown skill"</li>
<li>Fixed plan mode asking for re-approval after the plan was already accepted</li>
<li>Fixed voice mode swallowing keypresses while a permission dialog or plan editor was open</li>
<li>Fixed <code>/voice</code> not working on Windows when installed via npm</li>
<li>Fixed spurious "Context limit reached" when invoking a skill with <code>model:</code> frontmatter on a 1M-context session</li>
<li>Fixed "adaptive thinking is not supported on this model" error when using non-standard model strings</li>
<li>Fixed <code>Bash(cmd:*)</code> permission rules not matching when a quoted argument contains <code>#</code></li>
<li>Fixed "don't ask again" in the Bash permission dialog showing the full raw command for pipes and compound commands</li>
<li>Fixed auto-compaction retrying indefinitely after consecutive failures — a circuit breaker now stops after 3 attempts</li>
<li>Fixed MCP reconnect spinner persisting after successful reconnection</li>
<li>Fixed LSP plugins not registering servers when the LSP Manager initialized before marketplaces were reconciled</li>
<li>Fixed clipboard copying in tmux over SSH — now attempts both direct terminal write and tmux clipboard integration</li>
<li>Fixed <code>/export</code> showing only the filename instead of the full file path in the success message</li>
<li>Fixed transcript not auto-scrolling to new messages after selecting text</li>
<li>Fixed Escape key not working to exit the login method selection screen</li>
<li>Fixed several Remote Control issues: sessions silently dying when the server reaps an idle environment, rapid messages being queued one-at-a-time instead of batched, and stale work items causing redelivery after JWT refresh</li>
<li>Fixed bridge sessions failing to recover after extended WebSocket disconnects</li>
<li>Fixed slash commands not found when typing the exact name of a soft-hidden command</li>
<li>Improved <code>--worktree</code> startup performance by reading git refs directly and skipping redundant <code>git fetch</code> when the remote branch is already available locally</li>
<li>Improved background agent behavior — killing a background agent now preserves its partial results in the conversation context</li>
<li>Improved model fallback notifications — now always visible instead of hidden behind verbose mode, with human-friendly model names</li>
<li>Improved blockquote readability on dark terminal themes — text is now italic with a left bar instead of dim</li>
<li>Improved stale worktree cleanup — worktrees left behind after an interrupted parallel run are now automatically cleaned up</li>
<li>Improved Remote Control session titles — now derived from your first prompt instead of showing "Interactive session"</li>
<li>Improved <code>/voice</code> to show your dictation language on enable and warn when your <code>language</code> setting isn't supported for voice input</li>
<li>Updated <code>--plugin-dir</code> to only accept one path to support subcommands — use repeated <code>--plugin-dir</code> for multiple directories</li>
<li>[VSCode] Fixed gitignore patterns containing commas silently excluding entire filetypes from the @-mention file picker</li>
</ul></div>
</div>
  <div data-view-component="true" class="Box-footer">

        <div data-pjax="true" data-test-selector="body-content" data-view-component="true" class="markdown-body tmp-my-3"><h2>What's changed</h2>
<ul>
<li>Added actionable suggestions to <code>/context</code> command — identifies context-heavy tools, memory bloat, and capacity warnings with specific optimization tips</li>
<li>Added <code>autoMemoryDirectory</code> setting to configure a custom directory for auto-memory storage</li>
<li>Fixed memory leak where streaming API response buffers were not released when the generator was terminated early, causing unbounded RSS growth on the Node.js/npm code path</li>
<li>Fixed managed policy <code>ask</code> rules being bypassed by user <code>allow</code> rules or skill <code>allowed-tools</code></li>
<li>Fixed full model IDs (e.g., <code>claude-opus-4-5</code>) being silently ignored in agent frontmatter <code>model:</code> field and <code>--agents</code> JSON config — agents now accept the same model values as <code>--model</code></li>
<li>Fixed MCP OAuth authentication hanging when the callback port is already in use</li>
<li>Fixed MCP OAuth refresh never prompting for re-auth after the refresh token expires, for OAuth servers that return errors with HTTP 200 (e.g. Slack)</li>
<li>Fixed voice mode silently failing on the macOS native binary for users whose terminal had never been granted microphone permission — the binary now includes the <code>audio-input</code> entitlement so macOS prompts correctly</li>
<li>Fixed <code>SessionEnd</code> hooks being killed after 1.5 s on exit regardless of <code>hook.timeout</code> — now configurable via <code>CLAUDE_CODE_SESSIONEND_HOOKS_TIMEOUT_MS</code></li>
<li>Fixed <code>/plugin install</code> failing inside the REPL for marketplace plugins with local sources</li>
<li>Fixed marketplace update not syncing git submodules — plugin sources in submodules no longer break after update</li>
<li>Fixed unknown slash commands with arguments silently dropping input — now shows your input as a warning</li>
<li>Fixed Hebrew, Arabic, and other RTL text not rendering correctly in Windows Terminal, conhost, and VS Code integrated terminal</li>
<li>Fixed LSP servers not working on Windows due to malformed file URIs</li>
<li>Changed <code>--plugin-dir</code> so local dev copies now override installed marketplace plugins with the same name (unless that plugin is force-enabled by managed settings)</li>
<li>[VSCode] Fixed delete button not working for Untitled sessions</li>
<li>[VSCode] Improved scroll wheel responsiveness in the integrated terminal with terminal-aware acceleration</li>
</ul></div>
</div>
  <div data-view-component="true" class="Box-footer">
        <div class="tmp-mb-3">

        <div data-pjax="true" data-test-selector="body-content" data-view-component="true" class="markdown-body tmp-my-3"><h2>What's changed</h2>
<ul>
<li>Added <code>modelOverrides</code> setting to map model picker entries to custom provider model IDs (e.g. Bedrock inference profile ARNs)</li>
<li>Added actionable guidance when OAuth login or connectivity checks fail due to SSL certificate errors (corporate proxies, <code>NODE_EXTRA_CA_CERTS</code>)</li>
<li>Fixed freezes and 100% CPU loops triggered by permission prompts for complex bash commands</li>
<li>Fixed a deadlock that could freeze Claude Code when many skill files changed at once (e.g. during <code>git pull</code> in a repo with a large <code>.claude/skills/</code> directory)</li>
<li>Fixed Bash tool output being lost when running multiple Claude Code sessions in the same project directory</li>
<li>Fixed subagents with <code>model: opus</code>/<code>sonnet</code>/<code>haiku</code> being silently downgraded to older model versions on Bedrock, Vertex, and Microsoft Foundry</li>
<li>Fixed background bash processes spawned by subagents not being cleaned up when the agent exits</li>
<li>Fixed <code>/resume</code> showing the current session in the picker</li>
<li>Fixed <code>/ide</code> crashing with <code>onInstall is not defined</code> when auto-installing the extension</li>
<li>Fixed <code>/loop</code> not being available on Bedrock/Vertex/Foundry and when telemetry was disabled</li>
<li>Fixed SessionStart hooks firing twice when resuming a session via <code>--resume</code> or <code>--continue</code></li>
<li>Fixed JSON-output hooks injecting no-op system-reminder messages into the model's context on every turn</li>
<li>Fixed voice mode session corruption when a slow connection overlaps a new recording</li>
<li>Fixed Linux sandbox failing to start with "ripgrep (rg) not found" on native builds</li>
<li>Fixed Linux native modules not loading on Amazon Linux 2 and other glibc 2.26 systems</li>
<li>Fixed "media_type: Field required" API error when receiving images via Remote Control</li>
<li>Fixed <code>/heapdump</code> failing on Windows with <code>EEXIST</code> error when the Desktop folder already exists</li>
<li>Improved Up arrow after interrupting Claude — now restores the interrupted prompt and rewinds the conversation in one step</li>
<li>Improved IDE detection speed at startup</li>
<li>Improved clipboard image pasting performance on macOS</li>
<li>Improved <code>/effort</code> to work while Claude is responding, matching <code>/model</code> behavior</li>
<li>Improved voice mode to automatically retry transient connection failures during rapid push-to-talk re-press</li>
<li>Improved the Remote Control spawn mode selection prompt with better context</li>
<li>Changed default Opus model on Bedrock, Vertex, and Microsoft Foundry to Opus 4.6 (was Opus 4.1)</li>
<li>Deprecated <code>/output-style</code> command — use <code>/config</code> instead. Output style is now fixed at session start for better prompt caching</li>
<li>VSCode: Fixed HTTP 400 errors for users behind proxies or on Bedrock/Vertex with Claude 4.5 models</li>
</ul></div>
</div>
  <div data-view-component="true" class="Box-footer">
        <div class="tmp-mb-3">

  <div data-view-component="true" class="Box-body">      <div class="d-flex flex-md-row flex-column">
  <div class="d-flex flex-row flex-1 tmp-mb-3 wb-break-word">
    <div class="flex-1" data-pjax="#repo-content-pjax-container" data-turbo-frame="repo-content-turbo-frame">
        <span data-view-component="true" class="tmp-mr-3 f1 text-bold d-inline"><a href="/anthropics/claude-code/releases/tag/v2.1.72" data-view-component="true" class="Link--primary Link">v2.1.72</a></span>
      <span>
        
          <div class="ml-2 d-none d-md-inline">
              

          </div>
      </span>
    </div>

    <div class="tmp-mt-3 ml-2 d-md-none">

        </div>

  </div>

        <div data-pjax="true" data-test-selector="body-content" data-view-component="true" class="markdown-body tmp-my-3"><h2>What's changed</h2>
<ul>
<li>Changed tool search to bypass the third-party proxy gate when the environment variable is set (replaces <code>CLAUDE_CODE_PROXY_SUPPORTS_TOOL_REFERENCE</code>, now removed)</li>
<li>Added <code>w</code> key in <code>/copy</code> to write the focused selection directly to a file, bypassing the clipboard (useful over SSH)</li>
<li>Added optional description argument to <code>/plan</code> (e.g., <code>/plan fix the auth bug</code>) that enters plan mode and immediately starts</li>
<li>Added <code>claude plugins</code> as an alias for <code>claude plugin</code></li>
<li>Added <code>ExitWorktree</code> tool to leave an <code>EnterWorktree</code> session</li>
<li>Added <code>CLAUDE_CODE_DISABLE_CRON</code> environment variable to immediately stop scheduled cron jobs mid-session</li>
<li>Added <code>lsof</code>, <code>pgrep</code>, <code>tput</code>, <code>ss</code>, <code>fd</code>, and <code>fdfind</code> to the bash auto-approval allowlist, reducing permission prompts for common read-only operations</li>
<li>Added support for marketplace git URLs without <code>.git</code> suffix (Azure DevOps, AWS CodeCommit)</li>
<li>Restored the <code>model</code> parameter on the Agent tool for per-invocation model overrides</li>
<li>Simplified effort levels to low/medium/high (removed max) with new symbols (○ ◐ ●) and a brief notification instead of a persistent icon. Use <code>/effort auto</code> to reset to default</li>
<li>Improved <code>/config</code> — Escape now cancels changes, Enter saves and closes, Space toggles settings</li>
<li>Improved up-arrow history to show current session's messages first when running multiple concurrent sessions</li>
<li>Improved voice input transcription accuracy for repo names and common dev terms (regex, OAuth, JSON)</li>
<li>Improved marketplace clone failure messages to show diagnostic info even when git produces no stderr</li>
<li>Improved <code>claude plugin validate</code> to explain that marketplace.json source paths are relative to the repo root when rejecting <code>../</code> paths</li>
<li>Improved bash command parsing by switching to a native module — faster initialization and no memory leak</li>
<li>Reduced false-positive bash permission prompts — tree-sitter parsing now handles <code>find -exec</code>, variable assignments, command substitutions, and many other patterns that previously triggered unnecessary prompts. Also fixed tree-sitter not loading in npm-installed versions</li>
<li>Reduced bundle size by ~510 KB</li>
<li>Changed CLAUDE.md HTML comments (<code>&lt;!-- ... --&gt;</code>) to be hidden from Claude when auto-injected. Comments remain visible when read with the Read tool</li>
<li>Fixed slow exits when background tasks or hooks were slow to respond</li>
<li>Fixed agent task progress stuck on "Initializing…"</li>
<li>Fixed skill hooks firing twice per event when a hooks-enabled skill is invoked by the model</li>
<li>Fixed several voice mode issues: occasional input lag, false "No speech detected" errors after releasing push-to-talk, and stale transcripts re-filling the prompt after submission</li>
<li>Fixed <code>--continue</code> not resuming from the most recent point after <code>--compact</code></li>
<li>Fixed bash security parsing edge cases</li>
<li>Fixed several plugin issues: installation failing on Windows with <code>EEXIST</code> error in OneDrive folders, marketplace blocking user-scope installs when a project-scope install exists, <code>CLAUDE_CODE_PLUGIN_CACHE_DIR</code> creating literal <code>~</code> directories, and <code>plugin.json</code> with marketplace-only fields failing to load</li>
<li>Fixed feedback survey appearing too frequently in long sessions</li>
<li>Fixed <code>--effort</code> CLI flag being reset by unrelated settings writes on startup</li>
<li>Fixed backgrounded Ctrl+B queries losing their transcript or corrupting the new conversation after <code>/clear</code></li>
<li>Fixed <code>/clear</code> killing background agent/bash tasks — only foreground tasks are now cleared</li>
<li>Fixed worktree isolation issues: Task tool resume not restoring cwd, and background task notifications missing <code>worktreePath</code> and <code>worktreeBranch</code></li>
<li>Fixed <code>/model</code> not displaying results when run while Claude is working</li>
<li>Fixed digit keys selecting menu options instead of typing in plan mode permission prompt's text input</li>
<li>Fixed sandbox permission issues: certain file write operations incorrectly allowed without prompting, and output redirections to allowlisted directories (like <code>/tmp/claude/</code>) prompting unnecessarily</li>
<li>Improved CPU utilization in long sessions</li>
<li>Fixed prompt cache invalidation in SDK <code>query()</code> calls, reducing input token costs up to 12x</li>
<li>Fixed Escape key becoming unresponsive after cancelling a query</li>
<li>Fixed double Ctrl+C not exiting when background agents or tasks are running</li>
<li>Fixed team agents to inherit the leader's model</li>
<li>Fixed "Always Allow" saving permission rules that never match again</li>
<li>Fixed several hooks issues: <code>transcript_path</code> pointing to the wrong directory for resumed/forked sessions, agent <code>prompt</code> being silently deleted from settings.json on every settings write, PostToolUse block reason displaying twice, async hooks not receiving stdin with bash <code>read -r</code>, and validation error message showing an example that fails validation</li>
<li>Fixed session crashes in Desktop/SDK when Read returned files containing U+2028/U+2029 characters</li>
<li>Fixed terminal title being cleared on exit even when <code>CLAUDE_CODE_DISABLE_TERMINAL_TITLE</code> was set</li>
<li>Fixed several permission rule matching issues: wildcard rules not matching commands with heredocs, embedded newlines, or no arguments; <code>sandbox.excludedCommands</code> failing with env var prefixes; "always allow" suggesting overly broad prefixes for nested CLI tools; and deny rules not applying to all command forms</li>
<li>Fixed oversized and truncated images from Bash data-URL output</li>
<li>Fixed a crash when resuming sessions that contained Bedrock API errors</li>
<li>Fixed intermittent "expected boolean, received string" validation errors on Edit, Bash, and Grep tool inputs</li>
<li>Fixed multi-line session titles when forking from a conversation whose first message contained newlines</li>
<li>Fixed queued messages not showing attached images, and images being lost when pressing ↑ to edit a queued message</li>
<li>Fixed parallel tool calls where a failed Read/WebFetch/Glob would cancel its siblings — only Bash errors now cascade</li>
<li>VSCode: Fixed scroll speed in integrated terminals not matching native terminals</li>
<li>VSCode: Fixed Shift+Enter submitting input instead of inserting a newline for users with older keybindings</li>
<li>VSCode: Added effort level indicator on the input border</li>
<li>VSCode: Added <code>vscode://anthropic.claude-code/open</code> URI handler to open a new Claude Code tab programmatically, with optional <code>prompt</code> and <code>session</code> query parameters</li>
</ul></div>
</div>
  <div data-view-component="true" class="Box-footer">

        <div data-pjax="true" data-test-selector="body-content" data-view-component="true" class="markdown-body tmp-my-3"><h2>What's changed</h2>
<ul>
<li>Added <code>/loop</code> command to run a prompt or slash command on a recurring interval (e.g. <code>/loop 5m check the deploy</code>)</li>
<li>Added cron scheduling tools for recurring prompts within a session</li>
<li>Added <code>voice:pushToTalk</code> keybinding to make the voice activation key rebindable in <code>keybindings.json</code> (default: space) — modifier+letter combos like <code>meta+k</code> have zero typing interference</li>
<li>Added <code>fmt</code>, <code>comm</code>, <code>cmp</code>, <code>numfmt</code>, <code>expr</code>, <code>test</code>, <code>printf</code>, <code>getconf</code>, <code>seq</code>, <code>tsort</code>, and <code>pr</code> to the bash auto-approval allowlist</li>
<li>Fixed stdin freeze in long-running sessions where keystrokes stop being processed but the process stays alive</li>
<li>Fixed a 5–8 second startup freeze for users with voice mode enabled, caused by CoreAudio initialization blocking the main thread after system wake</li>
<li>Fixed startup UI freeze when many claude.ai proxy connectors refresh an expired OAuth token simultaneously</li>
<li>Fixed forked conversations (<code>/fork</code>) sharing the same plan file, which caused plan edits in one fork to overwrite the other</li>
<li>Fixed the Read tool putting oversized images into context when image processing failed, breaking subsequent turns in long image-heavy sessions</li>
<li>Fixed false-positive permission prompts for compound bash commands containing heredoc commit messages</li>
<li>Fixed plugin installations being lost when running multiple Claude Code instances</li>
<li>Fixed claude.ai connectors failing to reconnect after OAuth token refresh</li>
<li>Fixed claude.ai MCP connector startup notifications appearing for every org-configured connector instead of only previously connected ones</li>
<li>Fixed background agent completion notifications missing the output file path, which made it difficult for parent agents to recover agent results after context compaction</li>
<li>Fixed duplicate output in Bash tool error messages when commands exit with non-zero status</li>
<li>Fixed Chrome extension auto-detection getting permanently stuck on "not installed" after running on a machine without local Chrome</li>
<li>Fixed <code>/plugin marketplace update</code> failing with merge conflicts when the marketplace is pinned to a branch/tag ref</li>
<li>Fixed <code>/plugin marketplace add owner/repo@ref</code> incorrectly parsing <code>@</code> — previously only <code>#</code> worked as a ref separator, causing undiagnosable errors with <code>strictKnownMarketplaces</code></li>
<li>Fixed duplicate entries in <code>/permissions</code> Workspace tab when the same directory is added with and without a trailing slash</li>
<li>Fixed <code>--print</code> hanging forever when team agents are configured — the exit loop no longer waits on long-lived <code>in_process_teammate</code> tasks</li>
<li>Fixed "❯ Tool loaded." appearing in the REPL after every <code>ToolSearch</code> call</li>
<li>Fixed prompting for <code>cd &lt;cwd&gt; &amp;&amp; git ...</code> on Windows when the model uses a mingw-style path</li>
<li>Improved startup time by deferring native image processor loading to first use</li>
<li>Improved bridge session reconnection to complete within seconds after laptop wake from sleep, instead of waiting up to 10 minutes</li>
<li>Improved <code>/plugin uninstall</code> to disable project-scoped plugins in <code>.claude/settings.local.json</code> instead of modifying <code>.claude/settings.json</code>, so changes don't affect teammates</li>
<li>Improved plugin-provided MCP server deduplication — servers that duplicate a manually-configured server (same command/URL) are now skipped, preventing duplicate connections and tool sets. Suppressions are shown in the <code>/plugin</code> menu.</li>
<li>Updated <code>/debug</code> to toggle debug logging on mid-session, since debug logs are no longer written by default</li>
<li>Removed startup notification noise for unauthenticated org-registered claude.ai connectors</li>
</ul></div>
</div>
  <div data-view-component="true" class="Box-footer">
        <div class="tmp-mb-3">
          <details-toggle>

      <summary role="button" data-target="details-toggle.summaryTarget" data-action="click:details-toggle#toggle" aria-expanded="false" data-view-component="true">    <span class="d-inline-flex flex-items-center">
      <span data-view-component="true" class="f3 text-bold ml-2 mr-2">Assets</span>
      <span title="2" data-view-component="true" class="Counter">2</span>
    </span>
</summary>
      <div data-view-component="true">      <include-fragment loading="lazy" src="https://github.com/anthropics/claude-code/releases/expanded_assets/v2.1.71" data-nonce="v2:82bc4f11-0cc3-1e7a-82a4-ac36f56c58ca" data-view-component="true">
  
        <span data-view-component="true">
  <svg style="box-sizing: content-box; color: var(--color-icon-primary);" width="32" height="32" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" aria-hidden="true" data-view-component="true" class="anim-rotate">

  <div data-view-component="true" class="Box-body">      <div class="d-flex flex-md-row flex-column">
  <div class="d-flex flex-row flex-1 tmp-mb-3 wb-break-word">
    <div class="flex-1" data-pjax="#repo-content-pjax-container" data-turbo-frame="repo-content-turbo-frame">
        <span data-view-component="true" class="tmp-mr-3 f1 text-bold d-inline"><a href="/anthropics/claude-code/releases/tag/v2.1.70" data-view-component="true" class="Link--primary Link">v2.1.70</a></span>

          <div class="ml-2 d-none d-md-inline">

  </div>

        <div data-pjax="true" data-test-selector="body-content" data-view-component="true" class="markdown-body tmp-my-3"><h2>What's changed</h2>
<ul>
<li>Fixed API 400 errors when using <code>ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL</code> with a third-party gateway — tool search now correctly detects proxy endpoints and disables <code>tool_reference</code> blocks</li>
<li>Fixed <code>API Error: 400 This model does not support the effort parameter</code> when using custom Bedrock inference profiles or other model identifiers not matching standard Claude naming patterns</li>
<li>Fixed empty model responses immediately after <code>ToolSearch</code> — the server renders tool schemas with system-prompt-style tags at the prompt tail, which could confuse models into stopping early</li>
<li>Fixed prompt-cache bust when an MCP server with <code>instructions</code> connects after the first turn</li>
<li>Fixed Enter inserting a newline instead of submitting when typing over a slow SSH connection</li>
<li>Fixed clipboard corrupting non-ASCII text (CJK, emoji) on Windows/WSL by using PowerShell <code>Set-Clipboard</code></li>
<li>Fixed extra VS Code windows opening at startup on Windows when running from the VS Code integrated terminal</li>
<li>Fixed voice mode failing on Windows native binary with "native audio module could not be loaded"</li>
<li>Fixed push-to-talk not activating on session start when <code>voiceEnabled: true</code> was set in settings</li>
<li>Fixed markdown links containing <code>#NNN</code> references incorrectly pointing to the current repository instead of the linked URL</li>
<li>Fixed repeated "Model updated to Opus 4.6" notification when a project's <code>.claude/settings.json</code> has a legacy Opus model string pinned</li>
<li>Fixed plugins showing as inaccurately installed in <code>/plugin</code></li>
<li>Fixed plugins showing "not found in marketplace" errors on fresh startup by auto-refreshing after marketplace installation</li>
<li>Fixed <code>/security-review</code> command failing with <code>unknown option merge-base</code> on older git versions</li>
<li>Fixed <code>/color</code> command having no way to reset back to the default color — <code>/color default</code>, <code>/color gray</code>, <code>/color reset</code>, and <code>/color none</code> now restore the default</li>
<li>Fixed a performance regression in the <code>AskUserQuestion</code> preview dialog that re-ran markdown rendering on every keystroke in the notes input</li>
<li>Fixed feature flags read during early startup never refreshing their disk cache, causing stale values to persist across sessions</li>
<li>Fixed <code>permissions.defaultMode</code> settings values other than <code>acceptEdits</code> or <code>plan</code> being applied in Claude Code Remote environments — they are now ignored</li>
<li>Fixed skill listing being re-injected on every <code>--resume</code> (~600 tokens saved per resume)</li>
<li>Fixed teleport marker not rendering in VS Code teleported sessions</li>
<li>Improved error message when microphone captures silence to distinguish from "no speech detected"</li>
<li>Improved compaction to preserve images in the summarizer request, allowing prompt cache reuse for faster and cheaper compaction</li>
<li>Improved <code>/rename</code> to work while Claude is processing, instead of being silently queued</li>
<li>Reduced prompt input re-renders during turns by ~74%</li>
<li>Reduced startup memory by ~426KB for users without custom CA certificates</li>
<li>Reduced Remote Control <code>/poll</code> rate to once per 10 minutes while connected (was 1–2s), cutting server load ~300×. Reconnection is unaffected — transport loss immediately wakes fast polling.</li>
<li>[VSCode] Added spark icon in VS Code activity bar that lists all Claude Code sessions, with sessions opening as full editors</li>
<li>[VSCode] Added full markdown document view for plans in VS Code, with support for adding comments to provide feedback</li>
<li>[VSCode] Added native MCP server management dialog — use <code>/mcp</code> in the chat panel to enable/disable servers, reconnect, and manage OAuth authentication without switching to the terminal</li>
</ul></div>
</div>

        <div data-pjax="true" data-test-selector="body-content" data-view-component="true" class="markdown-body tmp-my-3"><h2>What's changed</h2>
<ul>
<li>Added the <code>/claude-api</code> skill for building applications with the Claude API and Anthropic SDK</li>
<li>Added Ctrl+U on an empty bash prompt (<code>!</code>) to exit bash mode, matching <code>escape</code> and <code>backspace</code></li>
<li>Added numeric keypad support for selecting options in Claude's interview questions (previously only the number row above QWERTY worked)</li>
<li>Added optional name argument to <code>/remote-control</code> and <code>claude remote-control</code> (<code>/remote-control My Project</code> or <code>--name "My Project"</code>) to set a custom session title visible in claude.ai/code</li>
<li>Added Voice STT support for 10 new languages (20 total) — Russian, Polish, Turkish, Dutch, Ukrainian, Greek, Czech, Danish, Swedish, Norwegian</li>
<li>Added effort level display (e.g., "with low effort") to the logo and spinner, making it easier to see which effort setting is active</li>
<li>Added agent name display in terminal title when using <code>claude --agent</code></li>
<li>Added <code>sandbox.enableWeakerNetworkIsolation</code> setting (macOS only) to allow Go programs like <code>gh</code>, <code>gcloud</code>, and <code>terraform</code> to verify TLS certificates when using a custom MITM proxy with <code>httpProxyPort</code></li>
<li>Added <code>includeGitInstructions</code> setting (and <code>CLAUDE_CODE_DISABLE_GIT_INSTRUCTIONS</code> env var) to remove built-in commit and PR workflow instructions from Claude's system prompt</li>
<li>Added <code>/reload-plugins</code> command to activate pending plugin changes without restarting</li>
<li>Added a one-time startup prompt suggesting Claude Code Desktop on macOS and Windows (max 3 showings, dismissible)</li>
<li>Added <code>${CLAUDE_SKILL_DIR}</code> variable for skills to reference their own directory in SKILL.md content</li>
<li>Added <code>InstructionsLoaded</code> hook event that fires when CLAUDE.md or <code>.claude/rules/*.md</code> files are loaded into context</li>
<li>Added <code>agent_id</code> (for subagents) and <code>agent_type</code> (for subagents and <code>--agent</code>) to hook events</li>
<li>Added <code>worktree</code> field to status line hook commands with name, path, branch, and original repo directory when running in a <code>--worktree</code> session</li>
<li>Added <code>pluginTrustMessage</code> in managed settings to append organization-specific context to the plugin trust warning shown before installation</li>
<li>Added policy limit fetching (e.g., remote control restrictions) for Team plan OAuth users, not just Enterprise</li>
<li>Added <code>pathPattern</code> to <code>strictKnownMarketplaces</code> for regex-matching file/directory marketplace sources alongside <code>hostPattern</code> restrictions</li>
<li>Added plugin source type <code>git-subdir</code> to point to a subdirectory within a git repo</li>
<li>Added <code>oauth.authServerMetadataUrl</code> config option for MCP servers to specify a custom OAuth metadata discovery URL when standard discovery fails</li>
<li>Fixed a security issue where nested skill discovery could load skills from gitignored directories like <code>node_modules</code></li>
<li>Fixed trust dialog silently enabling all <code>.mcp.json</code> servers on first run. You'll now see the per-server approval dialog as expected</li>
<li>Fixed <code>claude remote-control</code> crashing immediately on npm installs with "bad option: --sdk-url" (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="3986490065" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/anthropics/claude-code/issues/28334" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/anthropics/claude-code/issues/28334/hovercard" href="https://github.com/anthropics/claude-code/issues/28334">#28334</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed <code>--model claude-opus-4-0</code> and <code>--model claude-opus-4-1</code> resolving to deprecated Opus versions instead of current</li>
<li>Fixed macOS keychain corruption when using multiple OAuth MCP servers. Large OAuth metadata blobs could overflow the <code>security -i</code> stdin buffer, silently leaving stale credentials behind and causing repeated <code>/login</code> prompts.</li>
<li>Fixed <code>.credentials.json</code> losing <code>subscriptionType</code> (showing "Claude API" instead of "Claude Pro"/"Claude Max") when the profile endpoint transiently fails during token refresh (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4013279626" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/anthropics/claude-code/issues/30185" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/anthropics/claude-code/issues/30185/hovercard" href="https://github.com/anthropics/claude-code/issues/30185">#30185</a>)</li>
<li>Fixed ghost dotfiles (<code>.bashrc</code>, <code>HEAD</code>, etc.) appearing as untracked files in the working directory after sandboxed Bash commands on Linux</li>
<li>Fixed Shift+Enter printing <code>[27;2;13~</code> instead of inserting a newline in Ghostty over SSH</li>
<li>Fixed stash (Ctrl+S) being cleared when submitting a message while Claude is working</li>
<li>Fixed ctrl+o (transcript toggle) freezing for many seconds in long sessions with lots of file edits</li>
<li>Fixed plan mode feedback input not supporting multi-line text entry (backslash+Enter and Shift+Enter now insert newlines)</li>
<li>Fixed cursor not moving down into blank lines at the top of the input box</li>
<li>Fixed <code>/stats</code> crash when transcript files contain entries with missing or malformed timestamps</li>
<li>Fixed a brief hang after a streaming error on long sessions (the transcript was being fully rewritten to drop one line; it is now truncated in place)</li>
<li>Fixed <code>--setting-sources user</code> not blocking dynamically discovered project skills</li>
<li>Fixed duplicate CLAUDE.md, slash commands, agents, and rules when running from a worktree nested inside its main repo (e.g. <code>claude -w</code>)</li>
<li>Fixed plugin Stop/SessionEnd/etc hooks not firing after any <code>/plugin</code> operation</li>
<li>Fixed plugin hooks being silently dropped when two plugins use the same <code>${CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT}/...</code> command template</li>
<li>Fixed memory leak in long-running SDK/CCR sessions where conversation messages were retained unnecessarily</li>
<li>Fixed API 400 errors in forked agents (autocompact, summarization) when resuming sessions that were interrupted mid-tool-batch</li>
<li>Fixed "unexpected tool_use_id found in tool_result blocks" error when resuming conversations that start with an orphaned tool result</li>
<li>Fixed teammates accidentally spawning nested teammates via the Agent tool's <code>name</code> parameter</li>
<li>Fixed <code>CLAUDE_CODE_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS</code> being ignored during conversation compaction</li>
<li>Fixed <code>/compact</code> summary rendering as a user bubble in SDK consumers (Claude Code Remote web UI, VSCode extension)</li>
<li>Fixed voice space bar getting stuck after a failed voice activation (module loading race, cold GrowthBook)</li>
<li>Fixed worktree file copy on Windows</li>
<li>Fixed global <code>.claude</code> folder detection on Windows</li>
<li>Fixed symlink bypass where writing new files through a symlinked parent directory could escape the working directory in <code>acceptEdits</code> mode</li>
<li>Fixed sandbox prompting users to approve non-allowed domains when <code>allowManagedDomainsOnly</code> is enabled in managed settings — non-allowed domains are now blocked automatically with no bypass</li>
<li>Fixed interactive tools (e.g., <code>AskUserQuestion</code>) being silently auto-allowed when listed in a skill's allowed-tools, bypassing the permission prompt and running with empty answers</li>
<li>Fixed multi-GB memory spike when committing with large untracked binary files in the working tree</li>
<li>Fixed Escape not interrupting a running turn when the input box has draft text. Use Up arrow to pull queued messages back for editing, or Ctrl+U to clear the input line.</li>
<li>Fixed Android app crash when running local slash commands (<code>/voice</code>, <code>/cost</code>) in Remote Control sessions</li>
<li>Fixed a memory leak where old message array versions accumulated in React Compiler <code>memoCache</code> over long sessions</li>
<li>Fixed a memory leak where REPL render scopes accumulated over long sessions (~35MB over 1000 turns)</li>
<li>Fixed memory retention in in-process teammates where the parent's full conversation history was pinned for the teammate's lifetime, preventing GC after <code>/clear</code> or auto-compact</li>
<li>Fixed a memory leak in interactive mode where hook events could accumulate unboundedly during long sessions</li>
<li>Fixed hang when <code>--mcp-config</code> points to a corrupted file</li>
<li>Fixed slow startup when many skills/plugins are installed</li>
<li>Fixed <code>cd &lt;outside-dir&gt; &amp;&amp; &lt;cmd&gt;</code> permission prompt to surface the chained command instead of only showing "Yes, allow reading from /"</li>
<li>Fixed conditional <code>.claude/rules/*.md</code> files (with <code>paths:</code> frontmatter) and nested CLAUDE.md files not loading in print mode (<code>claude -p</code>)</li>
<li>Fixed <code>/clear</code> not fully clearing all session caches, reducing memory retention in long sessions</li>
<li>Fixed terminal flicker caused by animated elements at the scrollback boundary</li>
<li>Fixed UI frame drops on macOS when using MCP servers with OAuth (regression from 2.1.x)</li>
<li>Fixed occasional frame stalls during typing caused by synchronous debug log flushes</li>
<li>Fixed <code>TeammateIdle</code> and <code>TaskCompleted</code> hooks to support <code>{"continue": false, "stopReason": "..."}</code> to stop the teammate, matching <code>Stop</code> hook behavior</li>
<li>Fixed <code>WorktreeCreate</code> and <code>WorktreeRemove</code> plugin hooks being silently ignored</li>
<li>Fixed skill descriptions with colons (e.g., "Triggers include: X, Y, Z") failing to load from SKILL.md frontmatter</li>
<li>Fixed project skills without a <code>description:</code> frontmatter field not appearing in Claude's available skills list</li>
<li>Fixed <code>/context</code> showing identical token counts for all MCP tools from a server</li>
<li>Fixed literal <code>nul</code> file creation on Windows when the model uses CMD-style <code>2&gt;nul</code> redirection in Git Bash</li>
<li>Fixed extra blank lines appearing below each tool call in the expanded subagent transcript view (Ctrl+O)</li>
<li>Fixed Tab/arrow keys not cycling Settings tabs when <code>/config</code> search box is focused but empty</li>
<li>Fixed service key OAuth sessions (CCR containers) spamming <code>[ERROR]</code> logs with 403s from profile-scoped endpoints</li>
<li>Fixed inconsistent color for "Remote Control active" status indicator</li>
<li>Fixed Voice waveform cursor covering the first suffix letter when dictating mid-input</li>
<li>Fixed Voice input showing all 5 spaces during warmup instead of capping at ~2 (aligning with the "keep holding…" hint)</li>
<li>Improved spinner performance by isolating the 50ms animation loop from the surrounding shell, reducing render and CPU overhead during turns</li>
<li>Improved UI rendering performance in native binaries with React Compiler</li>
<li>Improved <code>--worktree</code> startup by eliminating a git subprocess on the startup path</li>
<li>Improved macOS startup by eliminating redundant settings-file reloads when managed settings resolve</li>
<li>Improved macOS startup for Claude.ai enterprise/team users by skipping an unnecessary keychain lookup</li>
<li>Improved MCP <code>-p</code> startup by pipelining claude.ai config fetch with local connections and using a concurrency pool instead of sequential batching</li>
<li>Improved voice startup by removing imperceptible warmup pulse animations that were causing re-render stutter</li>
<li>Improved MCP binary content handling: tools returning PDFs, Office documents, or audio now save decoded bytes to disk wit...</li>
</ul></div>
          <a href="/anthropics/claude-code/releases/tag/v2.1.69" data-view-component="true" class="Link">Read more</a>
</div>

        <div data-pjax="true" data-test-selector="body-content" data-view-component="true" class="markdown-body tmp-my-3"><h2>What's changed</h2>
<ul>
<li>Opus 4.6 now defaults to medium effort for Max and Team subscribers. Medium effort works well for most tasks — it's the sweet spot between speed and thoroughness. You can change this anytime with <code>/model</code></li>
<li>Re-introduced the "ultrathink" keyword to enable high effort for the next turn</li>
<li>Removed Opus 4 and 4.1 from Claude Code on the first-party API — users with these models pinned are automatically moved to Opus 4.6</li>
</ul></div>
